    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

        if (this.up('#box')) {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });

<span id="freeTextContainer6606174343453886337">I got 'Lift' by Raymond Wheeler for my boyfriend. He is the manager of a popular restaurant but had found the morale and motivation of his staff had dropped significantly during the Covid-19 pandemic. With uncertainty over their future and being face with an almost unbearable surge in business during Eat Out to Help Out and then an unavoidable cut in hours, the performance and willingness of his staff were at an all-time low.<br/>He read 'Lift' and found it to be so useful in learning how to better c</span>
  <span id="freeText6606174343453886337" style="display:none">I got 'Lift' by Raymond Wheeler for my boyfriend. He is the manager of a popular restaurant but had found the morale and motivation of his staff had dropped significantly during the Covid-19 pandemic. With uncertainty over their future and being face with an almost unbearable surge in business during Eat Out to Help Out and then an unavoidable cut in hours, the performance and willingness of his staff were at an all-time low.<br />He read 'Lift' and found it to be so useful in learning how to better communicate with his staff, and how to encourage his staff to communicate their concerns to him, building an environment of trust. As opposed to the atmosphere of doom and gloom, there is a feeling of hope in his staff, even during these difficult times. This has built up the morale of his staff and improved relationships and interactions with customers.</span>

<div id="review_3636385605" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3636385605" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3636385605?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3636385605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11673914125200006005">‘Enjoy the benefit of higher productivity and morale’<br/><br/>Oregon author Raymond L. Wheeler earned his MA in Intercultural Studies from Fuller Theological Seminary, his Doctor of Ministry from Claremont School of Theology, and worked in business and ministry, and after retiring from being an executive coach and pastor, he is an adjunct professor of research and ministry at LIFE Pacific University in San Dimas, California as well as an author. His initial book was CHANGE THE PARADIGM: HOW TO LEAD LIKE </span>
  <span id="freeText11673914125200006005" style="display:none">‘Enjoy the benefit of higher productivity and morale’<br /><br />Oregon author Raymond L. Wheeler earned his MA in Intercultural Studies from Fuller Theological Seminary, his Doctor of Ministry from Claremont School of Theology, and worked in business and ministry, and after retiring from being an executive coach and pastor, he is an adjunct professor of research and ministry at LIFE Pacific University in San Dimas, California as well as an author. His initial book was CHANGE THE PARADIGM: HOW TO LEAD LIKE JESUS IN TODAY’S WORLD. Now he offers LIFT: FIVE PRACTICES GREAT MANAGERS DO CONSISTENTLY. <br /><br />As stated on a website, ‘Great managers build high performance by consistently building ownership, working facts, knowing their people and themselves, managing activities, and building a climate of hope. In contrast, besieged managers tend to be more dictatorial, emotionally unpredictable, lacking in self-awareness, consumed with employee failures, and cynical…LIFT offers a way forward for anyone looking to improve the way they manage their team.’ That statement succinctly distills the goal – and achievement - of this excellent book.<br /><br />In his introductory comments, Dr. Wheeler offers the following: ‘What makes great managers so successful? I set about to interview successful managers across several industries including financial services, health care, religious non-profit, hospitality software, manufacturing, and insides sales. …I was delighted to find that the five practices my inquires uncovered worked in lifting employee performance, I was surprised to see how challenging putting these practices to work was in helping me be a better manager…this book is an attempt to define situationally tested methods that make a difference in how employees engage their work and perform…’<br /><br />The five practices so thoroughly and accessibly discussed are Create Ownership and not a Dictatorship, Work Facts not Emotion, Know Your People and Yourself, Manage Activities not Results, and Build Climate of Hope, not Cynicism. The manner in which each of this ‘lifts’ are presented with excellent tables, footnotes, appendices and references, and a series of interviewed situations makes this book not only accessible to read, but also immediately available for incorporating into action for the receptive mangers fortunate enough for this exposure. This is a very fine book by an engaging and caring author! Recommended<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11673914125200006005" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3659505458" class="review notext" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IPOOQacZJnt88kw05ThJJ4af31eO+IuMw0CYoWV6JylbQwKp28Jr79HHonrpe1QpldJnJ71yxfrOoeb+uP9Luw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FiG+4YDrcfJZ+LOaml5G3AwfJv/DgLyLoyB7T+aJh7ttkTIJ/DA8ZvTNXdSWHVvSH1Kej/AK8v2uwQUQOwzrKQ==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer11167733989055497222">Raymond L Wheeler is a retired certified executive coach, leadership development consultant, and ordained pastoral leader. He continues to work with leaders in the complexities of a rapidly changing workplace as a friend and mentor. <br/>Ray's diverse experience in business (operations, administration, and sales) and ministry (campus pastor, lead pastor, executive pastor, church planting coach, world m</span>
  <span id="freeText11167733989055497222" style="display:none">Raymond L Wheeler is a retired certified executive coach, leadership development consultant, and ordained pastoral leader. He continues to work with leaders in the complexities of a rapidly changing workplace as a friend and mentor. <br />Ray's diverse experience in business (operations, administration, and sales) and ministry (campus pastor, lead pastor, executive pastor, church planting coach, world missions) means he understands leaders' challenges. He has also worked as a denominational executive and radio personality (formerly KFSG in Los Angeles). Ray is an adjunct professor in ministry, research methods, teaching methods, leadership, and leadership ethics for LIFE Pacific University in San Dimas, California, and adjunct professor of leadership at International Theological Seminary in Covina, California. Ray and Janice (his wife of 46 years) have three adult children and four grandchildren. He holds a Master of Arts in Intercultural Studies from Fuller Theological Seminary and a Doctor of Ministry in Administration and Leadership from Claremont School of Theology. <br />Ray is the author of Change the Paradigm: How to Lead Like Jesus in Today's World (2015) and Lift: five practices great managers do consistently (2020).<br />Ray serves on the board for Hospitality International Services. <br />Getting to know Ray is inspiring and fun. Working with Ray is a chance to raise the bar in performance and accomplishment. <br /></span>
